 Kern said this is the sixth model after the S, E, C, ML and GL classes to be built at the company's Chakan plant

 90 lakh rupainput bhashaa se England's most successful Test bowler James Anderson has been ruled out of the second Ashes Test with Australia on August 14 at Lord's due to a Coul injury (a calf injury)
 paanch maichon kii siries main australia ne abhi 1-0 kii badhat bana rakhi he
 Australia beat the hosts by 251 runs in Birmingham
 anderson us match main sirf chaar over gendbaaji kar sake the
 He was forced to go out of the ground for treatment due to the Kolph injury
 vah ballebaaji ke liye laute the, lekin ab england evam wales cricket board ne saaf kar diya he ki 37 saal ke anderson lords main nahin khel paaenge
 The ECB said in its statement, "he will go for rehabilitation due to injury
 iske liye lankashair or england team ke medical visheshgyon kii salaah lee jaaegi
 Based on this, we will free him to play further in the series
 'maidan par pollard kii is harakat se ICC khafa- laga jurmaana, mila dimerit pointapako bataa den ki nathan leone (49 / 6) or pat kamins (32 / 4) kii ghaatak gendbaaji ke dam par australia ne edbeston cricket maidan par khele gaye ashes siries ke pehle test match ke paanchaven or antim din somvaar ko england ko 251 ranon se rond daalaa
 Australian legend Steve Smith was the Player of the Match, scoring centuries (144, 142) in both innings
 ashes siries kaa doosraa test match 14 agast se lords main khelaa jayega
 With this, Australia took a 1-0 lead in the five-match series
 england ko match jeetne ke liye 398 ran banane the, lekin mejabaan team apni kharaab ballebaaji ke kaaran 52
 All out for 146 in 3 overs
 is maidan par australia kii 2001 ke baad se yah pehali jeet he
 Troubled by her husband not bathing and shaving for seven-eight days, the wife has approached the Family Court seeking divorce
 25 varshiya yuvak or 23 varshiya mahila kaa kareeb ek saal pehle hi vivaah hua he
 Shail Awasthi, counselor of Bhopal Kutumb Court, said, "the couple has filed a case in Kutumb Court here for divorce by mutual consent
" bhopal kutumb nyaayalay ke nyaayadhish aar en chand ne haal hi main is danpati ko nirdesh diye hai ki yadi unhen talaak chahie to agle chah maheene tak donon ko alag-alag rahanaa hoga
 After this, they will be given a certificate of divorce
 ''shail ne kaha, ‘‘mahila kaa kahana he ki lagaataar nahin nahaane ke kaaran uske pati ke sharir se badboo aati he or yadi nahaane ke liye kaha jaataa he to vah sharir evam kapadon par itr laga isse nijaat kii koshish karata he
 "shell said that" this is a month old case
 yah talaak final ho gaya he
 a case has been filed in the Kutumb court under the Hindu Marriage Act 13B by marriage with mutual consent and after six months the divorce of these couple will be duly done
 ''unhone kaha, ‘‘is danpati ke vivaah ko ek saal se upar ho gaya he
 It was the intercast marriage and the orange marriage
 ladkaa sindhi samaaj kaa he, jabaki ladki brahman samaaj kii he
 They do not have children
 ladkaa bairagarh main dukaan chalaata he
 She said that the woman said that after marriage she somehow tried to mold herself in the Sindhi family for a few days in their food and living, but she could not change herself in this family
 shail ne bataaya ki is ladki kaa aarope tha ki uske pati ke ghar main saamaan suvyavasthit dhang se rakhane kii bajaay idhar-udhar bikharaa rahata he
 The woman also has objections to this, her husband is not saving money for the future
 input- bhashaa Entrepreneur Neera Radia, who is lobbying companies, appeared as a prosecution witness in a special court in Delhi, hearing the 2G case
 unhone adaalat main pehali baar pesh hokar kaha ki unhen lagata he ki swaan telecom privet limited 2ji spectrum license paane kii paatr nahin thi kyonki yah company kathith taur par yah reliance adieji samooh kii company reliance communications se judi thi
 Radia stated during her testimony that at the time of allocation of 2008 2G spectrum there was a strong general perception that Swan Telecom Private Limited (STPL) does not qualify for spectrum allocation
 astipiel ke pravartak shahid osman balava or vinod goyanka par is maamle main abhiyukt he or un par isi adaalat main mukadmaa chal rahaa he
 Radia told Special CBI court Judge OP Saini, "at the time of allocation of spectrum, media had created a strong feeling in the minds of common people about eligibility and ineligibility"
 aam dharna or tata samooh ke vakeelon kii salaah ke jariye mujhe pataa chalaa ki yah company (swaan telecom) paatr nahin he
 During the process of recording the statements of the witnesses, he asked the CBI counsel in the court that at the time of allotment of licenses, such information was circulated that Swan Telecom Pvt Ltd was associated with Reliance Communications
 unhone kaha, haalanki iske bare main mere paas koi pukhta yaa vyaktigat jaankaree nahin thi
 Radia said that his public relations company used to advise the Tata group on telecom matters and Tata Teleservices Limited (TTSL) applied for a dual technology license in 2007
 radia ne adaalat se kaha ki titisel ko 2008 main dohari praudyogiki ke liye license pradaan kiya gaya tha, lekin use spectrum nahin mila
 Radia '' TTSL was advised that they were in the queue and would be given spectrum if available
 main tata samooh ke doorsanchaar maamle main samanvay kaa kaam kar rahi thi par main is kaam ko akele nahin kar rahi thi
 TTSL also applied for dual technology in the Delhi service sector
 is maamle main sibiai ke vakil ne radia se kaha, kya aap adaalat ko bataa sakati hai ki dilli seva kshetra main dohari praudyogiki vaale spectrum praapt karne ke maamle main titisel qatari main koun se number par thi
 In response to this question, Radia said, "I don't know what number she was in the case of getting dual technology spectrum in Delhi service area
" haalanki tata samooh or doorsanchaar vibhaag ke bich paryaapt patrachaar hua tha jisamen kaha gaya tha ki dohari praudyogki ke license hasil hone ke kaaran company qatari main aage he
 The company was already operating the CDMA service at that time
 sibiai ke pravaktaa ne radia se yah bataane ke liye kaha ki anya aavedakon se aage hone ke baavjood titisel ko dilli seva kshetra main 2ji spectrum kyon nahin mila
 He said, TTSL did not get spectrum earlier as dot said it was not ahead of other companies
 titisel ko yah baat doorsanchaar vibhaag ne maukhik taur par bataai thi
 Swan Telecom got spectrum in Delhi service area
 reliance communications ko bhi spectrum mila tha
 Radia also told the court that TTSL had opposed allocation of spectrum to Swan Telecom and Reliance Communications, but was advised to remain in the queue and get them whenever spectrum is available
 adaalat ne ab unke bayaan ko record karne kii taarikh 2 july tay kii he
 In the charge sheet filed against telecom minister a Raja and others by the CBI on 2 April 2011, Radia was named as a prosecution witness in the case
 radia se 2 disambar ko sibiai ke gavaah ke taur par pesh hone ke liye kaha gaya tha or vah teen maheene baad adaalat main pesh huin
 He had asked for three months' time on the basis of surgery done due to neurological disease
 radia kaa bayaan isliye bhi mahatvapurn he ki unhone sibiai ke saamne aapraadhik dand samhit kii dhara 161 ke tahat jaanch ke dauraan record karaae gaye apane bayaan main kaha tha ki swaan telecom privet limited jis par abhi mukadmaa chal rahaa he, vah ekikrut seva kaa license praapt karne kii paatr nahin thi
 Radia said, about Swan Telecom, which was the only applicant for spectrum in Delhi circle, i would like to say that as per the provisions, Swan Telecom was not eligible to get the Integrated Services (UAS) license as an applicant
 unhone 21 disambar 2010 ko record bayaan main sibiai se kaha tha, jahaan tab meri samaj he iskaa puraa niyantran reliance communications ke paas tha
 The CBI had alleged in its chargesheet that Reliance Telecom Ltd, an accused in the case, used ineligible company Swan Telecom as its masked company to obtain licenses and expensive spectrum
 swaan telecom or iske pravartak shahid osman balava or vinod goyanka, artiel or reliance adieji ke teen sheersh kaaryakari - gautam doshi, surendra pipaara or hari nair par anya aropiyon ke saath is maamle main mukadmaa chal rahaa he
 During the investigation of the case, Radia told the CBI that he had spoken to DMK MP Kanimoi who is also an accused in the 2G case after the 2009 general election
 tippaniyan In a statement recorded by the CBI on 29 January 2011, Radia dismissed the allegation that he had approached Kanimozhi to get Raja to the telecom ministry in the cabinet
 radia ne kaha tha, kanimoi se dilli main hui charchaa ke dauraan hamane mantrimandal main dramuk ke sambhavit ummidavaaron par charchaa kii
 A
 Raja was not interested in the Telecom Ministry as far as i remember
 unhone sibiai ko bataaya tha ‘‘na maine e raja ko doorsanchaar mantralay dilaane ke liye kanimoi se sampark kiya tha na hi main itane bade jimme ke laayak thi
 She had told the CBI that the former telecom minister Dayanidhi Mara had caused major problems for the Tata group, so she was worried about his department as the Tata group was a customer of his public relations company Vaishnavi Corporate Communications Pvt Ltd
 radia ne apni gavaahi ke dauraan kaha ki 2008 2ji spectrum aavanton ke samay ek majboot aam dharna thi ki swaan telecom privet limited (astipiel) spectrum aavanton kii paatrata nahin rakhti
 The promoters of STPL, Shahid Usman Balwa and Vinod Goenka, are accused in the case and are being tried in this court
 radia ne vishesh sibiai adaalat ke nyaayadhish opi saini se kaha, spectrum aavanton ke samay media ne paatrata or apaatrata ke bare main aam logon ke man main ek drudh bhaavana paidaa kar di thi
 i came to know through common belief and advice from Tata group lawyers that this company (swan Telecom) is not eligible
 gavaahon ke bayaan darj kiye jane kii prakriya ke dauraan unhone sibiai ke vakil ke poochne par adaalat main kaha ki license aavanton ke samay aisi suchanaaen faili hui thim ki swaan telecom privet limited reliance communications se judi he
 He said, though i had no firm or personal information about it
 radia ne kaha ki unki jansampark company tata samooh ko doorsanchaar maamle main salaah detii thi or tata teleservices limited (titisel) ne 2007 main dohari praudyogiki license ke liye aavedan kiya tha
 Radia told the court that TTSL was granted a license for dual technology in 2008, but did not get spectrum
 radia ‘‘titisel ko salaah di gai thi ki ve qatari main hai or uplabdh hone par unhen spectrum diya jayega
 i was working in coordination with the Tata group in telecommunications, but i was not doing it alone
 titisel ne dohari praudyogiki ke liye dilli seva kshetra main bhi aavedan kiya tha
 In this case, the CBI lawyer told Radia, "can you tell the court which number in the queue TTSL was in the case of receiving dual technology spectrum in Delhi service area"
 is sawaal ke jawaab main radia ne kaha, mujhe yah nahin pataa ki dilli seva kshetra main dohari praudyogiki ke spectrum praapt karne ke maamle main vah kis number par thi
 However, there was substantial correspondence between the Tata group and the Department of Telecommunications stating that the company was ahead in the line due to dual technology licenses
 company us vakt sidime seva kaa parichaalan pehle se kar rahi thi
 a CBI spokesperson asked Radia to explain why TTSL did not get 2G spectrum in Delhi service area despite being ahead of other applicants
 unhone kaha, titisel ko pehle spectrum nahin mila kyonki doorsanchaar vibhaag ne kaha ki vah anya companiyon se aage nahin thi
 This was communicated verbally by dot to TTSL
 swaan telecom ko dilli seva kshetra main spectrum mila
 Reliance Communications also got spectrum
 radia ne adaalat se yah bhi kaha ki titisel ne swaan telecom or reliance communications ko spectrum ke aavanton kaa virodh kiya tha, lekin use salaah di gai ki qatari main bani rahe or jab bhi spectrum uplabdh hoga unhen mil jayega
 The court has now fixed July 2 for recording his statement
 sibiai ne 2 april 2011 ko duuranchaar mantri e raja or anya ke khilaaf daayar aaropapatr main is maamle main radia kaa naam abhiyojan paksh ke gavaah taur par darj kiya tha
 Radia was asked to appear as a CBI witness on 2 December and she appeared in court three months later
 unhone snaivik beemaari kii vajah se hui shalya chikitsa ke aadhaar par teen maheene kaa vakt maanga tha
 Radia's statement is also important because in his statement recorded during the investigation under Section 161 of Criminal Penal Code, before the CBI, he said that Swan Telecom Private Limited, which is currently under trial, is licensed for integrated service Was not eligible to do
 radia ne kaha, swaan telecom, jo dilli sarkal main spectrum ke liye iklauti aavedak thi, ke bare main kahana chaahuungi ki sabhi tarah praavdhaanon ke mutabik, aavedak ke taur par swaan telecom ekikrut seva (yueyes) license praapt karne kii paatr nahin thi
 He told the CBI in a record statement on December 21, 2010, where then i understand that Reliance Communications had full control over it
 sibiai ne apane aaropapatr main aarope lagaaya tha ki is maamle main aaropee reliance telecom limited ne license or mahange spectrum praapt karne ke liye apaatr company swaan telecom kaa upyog apni mukhauta company kii tarah kiya tha
 Swan Telecom and its promoters Shahid Usman Balwa and Vinod Goenka, RTL and Reliance adag's three top executive - Gautam Doshi, Surendra Pipara and Hari Nair, are being tried in the case along with other accused
 is maamle kii jaanch ke dauraan radia ne sibiai se kaha tha ki unhone 2009 aam chunaav ke baad dramuk saansad kanimoi se baat kii thi jo 2ji maamle main aaropee bhi hai
 The comments sibiai dwaara 29 janvari 2011 ko darj bayaan main radia ne is aarope ko khaarij kiya tha ki unhone mantrimandal main raja ko doorsanchaar mantralay dilaane ke liye kanimoi se sampark kiya tha
 Radia had said, during the discussion with Kanimozhi in Delhi, we discussed the possible DMK candidates in the cabinet
 jahaan tak mujhe yaad he e raja kii ruchi doorsanchaar mantralay main nahin thi
 He told the CBI, "neither did i contact Kanimozhi to get A
 Raja the telecom ministry, nor did i deserve such a big responsibility
" unhone sibiai se kaha tha ki ki purv doorsanchaar mantri dayaanidhi maarane ne tata samooh ke liye badi dikkatein paidaa kii thim isliye vah unke vibhaag ke bare main chintit thim kyonki tata samooh unki jansampark company vaishnavi copererat communications privet limited kii graahak thi

 However, there was substantial correspondence between the Tata group and the Department of Telecommunications stating that the company was ahead in the line due to dual technology licenses
 company us vakt sidime seva kaa parichaalan pehle se kar rahi thi
 a CBI spokesperson asked Radia to explain why TTSL did not get 2G spectrum in Delhi service area despite being ahead of other applicants
 unhone kaha, titisel ko pehle spectrum nahin mila kyonki doorsanchaar vibhaag ne kaha ki vah anya companiyon se aage nahin thi
 This was communicated verbally by dot to TTSL
 swaan telecom ko dilli seva kshetra main spectrum mila
 Reliance Communications also got spectrum
 radia ne adaalat se yah bhi kaha ki titisel ne swaan telecom or reliance communications ko spectrum ke aavanton kaa virodh kiya tha, lekin use salaah di gai ki qatari main bani rahe or jab bhi spectrum uplabdh hoga unhen mil jayega
 The court has now fixed July 2 for recording his statement
 sibiai ne 2 april 2011 ko duuranchaar mantri e raja or anya ke khilaaf daayar aaropapatr main is maamle main radia kaa naam abhiyojan paksh ke gavaah taur par darj kiya tha
 Radia was asked to appear as a CBI witness on 2 December and she appeared in court three months later
 unhone snaivik beemaari kii vajah se hui shalya chikitsa ke aadhaar par teen maheene kaa vakt maanga tha
 Radia's statement is also important because in his statement recorded during the investigation under Section 161 of Criminal Penal Code, before the CBI, he said that Swan Telecom Private Limited, which is currently under trial, is licensed for integrated service Was not eligible to do
 radia ne kaha, swaan telecom, jo dilli sarkal main spectrum ke liye iklauti aavedak thi, ke bare main kahana chaahuungi ki sabhi tarah praavdhaanon ke mutabik, aavedak ke taur par swaan telecom ekikrut seva (yueyes) license praapt karne kii paatr nahin thi
 He told the CBI in a record statement on December 21, 2010, where then i understand that Reliance Communications had full control over it
 sibiai ne apane aaropapatr main aarope lagaaya tha ki is maamle main aaropee reliance telecom limited ne license or mahange spectrum praapt karne ke liye apaatr company swaan telecom kaa upyog apni mukhauta company kii tarah kiya tha
 Swan Telecom and its promoters Shahid Usman Balwa and Vinod Goenka, RTL and Reliance adag's three top executive - Gautam Doshi, Surendra Pipara and Hari Nair, are being tried in the case along with other accused
 is maamle kii jaanch ke dauraan radia ne sibiai se kaha tha ki unhone 2009 aam chunaav ke baad dramuk saansad kanimoi se baat kii thi jo 2ji maamle main aaropee bhi hai

 Raja the telecom ministry, nor did i deserve such a big responsibility

 tippaniyan In a statement recorded by the CBI on 29 January 2011, Radia dismissed the allegation that he had approached Kanimozhi to get Raja to the telecom ministry in the cabinet

 'bhartiya agenciyaan maanati he ki afghanistan ke ‘chuninda kshetra’ 2016 se hi bharat ke radar par hai

 inamen 17 kasargod or 4 palakkad jile ke rahane vaale the

 bataa den ki bharat se ISIS main shaamil hone ke iraade se afghanistan yaa iraq pahunchane ke liye yuvak iran ke raste kaa istemaal karte rahe hai
 This is despite Iran's tough stand on ISIS
 rashtriya jaanch agency (enie) ne iske peeche ke napak khel ko benakaab kiya
 Nearly two dozen suspected ISIS operatives, most of whom were from Kerala, used the Iranian route to foster Indian agencies
 india today ne is sambandh main vynad jile ke kalpetta main rahane vaale nashidul hamajafar ke root ko trek kiya
 Nasheedul was the first suspect who was deported from Afghanistan to India last year
 sitambar-oktober 2017 main kabhi nashidul vynad se oman kii rajdhani muscat pahunchaa
 On 13 October 2017, he left the Emirates flight to Tehran from Muscat International Airport with his colleague Habib
 nashidul ne habib ke passport ke jariye airport par irani simcard liya
 Then he took room on Imam Khomeini Street
 vahaan wo apane ISIS contact person ke nirdesh kaa intazaar karne laga
 There was a directive on the cryptic messaging app 'telegram' to go to Afghanistan Embassy for a visa for Afghanistan
 sutron ne bataaya ki nashidul or habib phir afgaan duutavas gaye, jahaan unka intervyuu hua
 He was asked to visit the embassy three days later
 unhen kaha gaya ki visa bhartiya duutavas se ‘no objection certificate’ milane ke baad process kar diya jayega
 Nasidul and Habib did not go to the Indian Embassy for fear of being caught
 nashidul aies oparative banane ke liye ada tha lekin uskaa sahyogi habib apane pita se sampark karne ke baad kerala ghar lautne ke liye ravaanaa ho gaya
 Nasheedul then reached the city of Isfahan in Iran by traveling 450 km by taxi
 sutron ke mutabik nashidul ne bharat main poochtacha karne waalon ko bataaya ki chah ghante ke thakaane vaale is taxi ke safar ke liye usne 100 dollar die
 The isex's Kantex person arrived late last night to meet Nasheedul
 usne nashidul ke saamaan kii talaashi lee or uskaa laptop, yphone or passport le liya

 iske baad guide ne nashidul se 450 america dollar (kareeb 32000 bhartiya rupye) afghanistan main iesas ke kshetra pahunchane kii fees ke taur par vasule

 nashidul ke mutabik usne agle din camp main lambii qatari dekhi

 vahaan use pakistani hone ke andeh main us vaahan par chadha diya gaya, jisamen pakistan deport kiye jane vaale log savaar the

 is par nashidul ko waapas afgaan camp bhej diya gaya

 haalanki baad main afgaan or america intelegence agenciyon ne use hiraasat main lekar poochtacha kii

 Now the Foreign Minister of Iran has threatened many countries, including India, on the shift of ISIS base to Afghanistan
 sutron ne india today ko bataaya ki bhartiya agenciyaan is ghatnakram ko lekar puri tarah chaukas hai
 Operation 'jackpot' ended in just 15 minutes; Baghdadi caused worldwide devastation in 5 years
 Abu's companion was caught in February last year, preparations for mission abolition; Already happened
 america ne uske khatme ke liye mishan ablitaryshan kii kahani kareeb dedh saal pehle hi likh lee thi or sahi samay kaa intjaar kar rahaa tha
 This special operation carried out at night was named Mission Abolition and the codename of terrorist Baghdadi was Operation Jackpot
 sirf 2 baar dikhaai diya bagdadeepichley 5 saalon main khooni sanghathan iesas par bagdadi kaa kabja rahaa or isane is dauraan duniya ko jahannum banane main koi kasar nahin chodi
 But in these last 5 years it was neither easy to get information about Abu Bakr al-baghdadi nor to capture it
 in 5 saalon main bagdadi dikhaa to sirf 2 baar magar uski aawaaj or uske aatanki duniya main dehshat machaate rahe

 bagdadi ko thikaane lagane kii kavayad shuru hoti he farvari 2018 se
 post-operation View on Baghdadi (AP) caught last year Baghdadi's partner In February 2018, Turkey's Armed Force captured Commander Ismail al-itthavi, Baghdadi's closest and special partner, while entering the country from border areas
 al ithavi ko giraftaar kar turki ne use iraq ko saunp diya
 It was not only the Iraqi army's eye on Etawi but the US military was also looking for it
 giraftaar ke baad ithavi ne bagdadi ke saare raaj kholkar rakh die the

 khufia agenciyon kii najaron se bachane ke liye wo aksar subjiyon se bhari mini trek main baithkar safar karata tha jisaki vajah se wo checking se har baar batch jaataa tha

 5 maheene pehle yani may 2019 main oparation kil bagdadi kii jimmedaari siie ne apane upar le lee or lagaataar pichley 5 maheene se bagdadi or uske ghar ko jasuson ke alaava satellite or drone kii madad se follow kiya ja rahaa tha

 jinhone isi imaarat main bagdadi ke hone kii baat ko conform kiya

 bagdadi ke guphanume bunker ko gher liya gaya

 taaki jameen main barood bichhe hone par ye robot morcha sambhaal lete

 kutton ne use daudaya

 is dhamaake main uske teen bete bhi maare gaye or imaarat jameendoj ho gai

 itnaa hi nahin, gupha main kuch aies aatankiyon ne sir par maut mandaraati dekh samarpan bhi kiya

 magar khud ko bam se udaane kii vajah se uske jism ke bhi chithde ud gaye

 It is alleged that the major Left parties in ticket distribution have ignored the interests of five smaller parties including Ghatak's All India Forward Bloc and Revolutionary Socialist Party (RSP)
 farward blaak or arsapi pashchim bengal sarkaar main shaamil hai

 vahiin 1977 main is vam dal ko 21 siton se santosh karnaa padaa
